< text>
I live down the street from this place and Valentines was our first time there. I have delayed eating their because of all the negative reviews. After work our little family just wanted to dine out and this was the closest especially because my husband and I were planning on having some wine.

Anyway it was a full house but once we got seated we got to look around and I have to say the openess of the restaurant is very nice. It allows energy to flow through the restaurant. Our server was nice and attentive.

Im giving this restaurant 2 stars because waiting for bread and oil took longer then we hoped it would (2nd round). I had to remind our server but she said the bread was in the oven. When we got our bread it was cold and I asked for balsamic vinegar, it never made it to the table. Receiving our appetizer (dumplings) it was cold, our server after waiting tells us that they were OUT of the appetizer my daughter wanted. So my daughter ordered another appetizer. Another 20 minutes later after bringing my main dish they expressed to my daughter again that they were out of those as well. I think its pretty pathetic! When a kitchen is out of something they should be update their servers. The kitchen sounded like they were unprepared for the amount of orders they had this night.

I ended up sharing my main dish with my kid because we didnt want to be there any longer then we already have. I was not pleased with how unorganize that place was. It was a turn off and now I realize why negative reviews are much nore critical because a bad experience can be the last experience you have at a franchise.

Anyway we were never compensated for the long wait, it sounds like it must happen often. It would of been nice if they offered us a free scoop of ice cream to make up for their incompetence.

Going back for just drinks, I DONT THINK SO. If you have 2 to 3 hours to spend to wait for food or to be told they are out after the fact that you wait 20 to 40 minutes to find out this is the place for you.

I had a Sangria (red) and it tasted more like fruit juice than wine. I have had Sangrias before but if you cant taste any alcohol, you are just sipping juice.</text>
